### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-400">檔案和頁面活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-400">File and page activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-401">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 的檔案和頁面活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-401">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-402">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-402">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-403">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-403">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-404">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-404">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-405">已存取檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-405">Accessed file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-406">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-406">FileAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-407">使用者或系統帳戶存取檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-407">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-408">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-408">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-409">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-409">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p150">這與「已存取檔案」(FileAccessed) 活動相關聯。當相同人員持續存取某個檔案一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p150">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity. A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p151">記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續存取某個檔案時，記錄 FileAccessed 事件的數目。這有助於減少多個 FileAccessed 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p151">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed. This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-414">已變更檔案的保留標籤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-414">Changed retention label for a file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-415">ComplianceSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-415">ComplianceSettingChanged</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p152">保留標籤已在文件中套用或移除。手動或自動將保留標籤套用到郵件時就會觸發此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p152">A retention label was applied to or removed from a document. This event is triggered when a retention label is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-418">已變更記錄狀態為鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-418">Changed record status to locked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-419">LockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-419">LockRecord</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p153">將文件歸類為記錄的保留標籤記錄狀態已鎖定。這表示文件無法修改或刪除。只有至少獲指派網站參與者權限的使用者可以變更文件記錄狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p153">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was locked. This means the document can't be modified or deleted. Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-423">已變更記錄狀態為解除鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-423">Changed record status to unlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-424">UnlockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-424">UnlockRecord</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p154">將文件歸類為記錄的保留標籤記錄狀態已解除鎖定。這表示文件可修改或刪除。只有至少獲指派網站參與者權限的使用者可以變更文件記錄狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p154">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was unlocked. This means that the document can be modified or deleted. Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-428">已簽入檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-428">Checked in file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-429">FileCheckedIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-429">FileCheckedIn</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-430">使用者簽入他們從文件庫簽出的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-430">User checks in a document that they checked out from a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-431">已簽出檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-431">Checked out file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-432">FileCheckedOut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-432">FileCheckedOut</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p155">使用者簽出位於文件庫中的文件。使用者可以簽出及變更與他們共用的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p155">User checks out a document located in a document library. Users can check out and make changes to documents that have been shared with them.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-435">已複製檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-435">Copied file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-436">FileCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-436">FileCopied</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p156">使用者複製網站中的文件。已複製的檔案可以儲存至該網站上的其他資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p156">User copies a document from a site. The copied file can be saved to another folder on the site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-439">已刪除檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-439">Deleted file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-440">FileDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-440">FileDeleted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-441">使用者刪除網站中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-441">User deletes a document from a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-442">已刪除資源回收筒中的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-442">Deleted file from recycle bin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-443">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-443">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-444">使用者從網站的資源回收筒中刪除檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-444">User deletes a file from the recycle bin of a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-445">已刪除第二階段資源回收筒中的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-445">Deleted file from second-stage recycle bin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-446">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-446">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-447">使用者從網站的第二階段資源回收筒中刪除檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-447">User deletes a file from the second-stage recycle bin of a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-448">標示為記錄的已刪除檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-448">Deleted file marked as a record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-449">RecordDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-449">RecordDelete</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p157">已刪除標示為記錄的文件。將會把內容標示為記錄的保留標籤套用至文件時，就會將文件視為記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p157">A document that was marked as a record was deleted. A document is considered a record when a retention label that marks content as a record is applied to the document.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-452">已偵測到文件敏感度不相符</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-452">Detected document sensitivity mismatch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-453">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-453">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p158">使用者將文件上傳到受敏感度標籤保護的網站，且文件的敏感度標籤優先於網站的敏感度標籤。例如，將套用「機密」標籤的文件上傳到套用「一般」標籤的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p158">User uploads a document to a site that's protected with a sensitivity label and the document has a higher priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site. For example, a document labeled Confidential is uploaded to a site labeled General. </span></span><br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p159">如果文件套用的敏感度標籤，其優先順序低於網站所套用的敏感度標籤，則不會觸發此事件。例如，將套用「一般」標籤的文件上傳到標記為「機密」的網站。如需敏感度標籤優先順序的詳細資訊，請參閱[標籤優先順序 (順序很重要)](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p159">This event isn't triggered if the document has a lower priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site. For example, a document labeled General is uploaded to a site labeled Confidential. For more information about sensitivity label priority, see [Label priority (order matters)](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-459">已偵測到檔案中的惡意程式碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-459">Detected malware in file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-460">FileMalwareDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-460">FileMalwareDetected</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-461">SharePoint 防毒引擎在檔案中偵測到惡意程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-461">SharePoint anti-virus engine detects malware in a file.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-462">已捨棄檔案簽出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-462">Discarded file checkout</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-463">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-463">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p160">使用者捨棄 (或復原) 已簽出的檔案。這表示會捨棄使用者在簽出時對檔案所做的任何變更，而且不會儲存至文件庫中的文件版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p160">User discards (or undoes) a checked out file. That means any changes they made to the file when it was checked out are discarded, and not saved to the version of the document in the document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-466">下載的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-466">Downloaded file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-467">FileDownloaded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-467">FileDownloaded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-468">使用者從網站下載文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-468">User downloads a document from a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-469">已修改檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-469">Modified file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-470">FileModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-470">FileModified</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-471">使用者或系統帳戶修改網站上的文件內容或屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-471">User or system account modifies the content or the properties of a document on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-472">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-472">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-473">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-473">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p161">這與「已修改檔案」(FileModified) 活動相關聯。當相同人員持續修改某個檔案一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p161">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity. A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p162">記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續修改某個檔案時，記錄 FileModified 事件的數目。這有助於減少多個 FileModified 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p162">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified. This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-478">已移動檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-478">Moved file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-479">FileMoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-479">FileMoved</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-480">使用者將文件從它在網站上目前的位置移動至新的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-480">User moves a document from its current location on a site to a new location.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-481">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-481">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-482">FilePreviewed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-482">FilePreviewed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p163">使用者預覽 SharePoint 或商務用 OneDrive 網站上的檔案。這些事件通常發生在單一活動中有龐大數量時，例如檢視影像資源庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p163">User previews files on a SharePoint or OneDrive for Business site. These events typically occur in high volumes based on a single activity, such as viewing an image gallery.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-485">已執行的搜尋查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-485">Performed search query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-486">SearchQueryPerformed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-486">SearchQueryPerformed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p164">使用者或系統帳戶在 SharePoint 或商務用 OneDrive 中執行搜尋。在服務帳戶執行搜尋查詢的一些常見案例，包含將電子文件探索保留和保留原則套用至網站和 OneDrive 帳戶，以及將保留或敏感度標籤自動套用至網站內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p164">User or system account performs a search in SharePoint or OneDrive for Business. Some common scenarios where a service account performs a search query include applying an eDiscovery holds and retention policy to sites and OneDrive accounts, and auto-applying retention or sensitivity labels to site content.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-489">已回收檔案的所有次要版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-489">Recycled all minor versions of file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-490">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-490">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p165">使用者從檔案的版本歷程記錄中刪除所有的次要版本。已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p165">User deletes all minor versions from the version history of a file. The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-493">已回收所有檔案版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-493">Recycled all versions of file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-494">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-494">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p166">使用者從檔案版本歷程記錄中刪除所有版本。已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p166">User deletes all versions from the version history of a file. The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-497">已回收檔案版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-497">Recycled version of file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-498">FileVersionRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-498">FileVersionRecycled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p167">使用者從檔案版本歷程記錄中刪除版本。已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p167">User deletes a version from the version history of a file. The deleted version is moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-501">已重新命名檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-501">Renamed file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-502">FileRenamed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-502">FileRenamed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-503">使用者重新命名網站上的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-503">User renames a document on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-504">已還原檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-504">Restored file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-505">FileRestored</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-505">FileRestored</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-506">使用者從網站的資源回收筒還原文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-506">User restores a document from the recycle bin of a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-507">已上傳檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-507">Uploaded file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-508">FileUploaded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-508">FileUploaded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-509">使用者將文件上傳至網站上的資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-509">User uploads a document to a folder on a site.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-510">已檢視頁面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-510">Viewed page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-511">PageViewed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-511">PageViewed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p168">使用者檢視網站上的檔案。這不包括使用網頁瀏覽器檢視文件庫中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p168">User views a page on a site. This doesn't include using a Web browser to view files located in a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-514">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-514">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-515">PageViewedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-515">PageViewedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p169">這與「已檢視頁面」(PageViewed) 活動相關聯。當相同人員持續檢視某個網頁一段時間 (最多 3 小時)，便會記錄 PageViewedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p169">This is related to the "Viewed page" (PageViewed) activity. A PageViewedExtended event is logged when the same person continually views a web page for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p170">記錄 PageViewedExtended 事件的目的在於減少持續檢視某個頁面時，記錄 PageViewed 事件的數目。這有助於減少多個 PageViewed 記錄的干擾，以了解哪些基本上是同樣的使用者活動，並讓您專注在初始 (且更重要的) PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p170">The purpose of logging PageViewedExtended events is to reduce the number of PageViewed events that are logged when a page is continually viewed. This helps reduce the noise of multiple PageViewed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) PageViewed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-520">用戶端發出的檢視訊號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-520">View signaled by client</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-521">ClientViewSignaled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-521">ClientViewSignaled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p171">使用者的用戶端 (例如網站或行動應用程式) 已發出訊號，指出使用者已檢視指示的頁面。此活動通常會在頁面的 PagePrefetched 事件之後進行記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p171">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has signaled that the indicated page has been viewed by the user. This activity is often logged following a PagePrefetched event for a page. </span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-p172">**注意**：由於 ClientViewSignaled 事件會由用戶端發出訊號，而不是由伺服器，所以伺服器可能不會記錄事件，因此事件可能也不會出現在稽核記錄中。稽核記錄中的資訊也可能不可靠。不過，因為用來建立訊號的權杖會驗證使用者的身分識別，因此對應稽核記錄中所列的使用者身分識別會是正確的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p172">**NOTE**: Because ClientViewSignaled events are signaled by the client, rather than the server, it's possible the event may not be logged by the server and therefore may not appear in the audit log. It's also possible that information in the audit record may not be trustworthy. However, because the user's identity is validated by the token used to create the signal, the user's identity listed in the corresponding audit record is accurate.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-527">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-527">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-528">PagePrefetched</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-528">PagePrefetched</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p173">使用者的用戶端 (例如網站或行動應用程式) 已要求指示的頁面在使用者瀏覽至此時，協助改善效能。記錄此事件的目的是指出頁面內容已對使用者的用戶端提供服務。此事件並非明確指示使用者已瀏覽到此頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p173">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has requested the indicated page to help improve performance if the user browses to it. This event is logged to indicate that the page content has been served to the user's client. This event isn't a definitive indication that the user navigated to the page.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p174">當用戶端呈現頁面內容時 (根據使用者的要求)，應該會隨即產生 ClientViewSignaled 事件。並非所有用戶端都支援指出預先擷取活動，因此某些預先擷取的活動可能會記錄為 PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p174">When the page content is rendered by the client (as per the user's request) a ClientViewSignaled event should be generated. Not all clients support indicating a pre-fetch, and therefore some pre-fetched activities might instead be logged as PageViewed events.</span></span>|
||||

#### <a name="frequently-asked-questions-about-fileaccessed-and-filepreviewed-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-534">FileAccessed 和 FilePreviewed 事件的常見問題集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-534">Frequently asked questions about FileAccessed and FilePreviewed events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-535">**任何非使用者事件是否能觸發包含使用者代理程式 (如 "OneDriveMpc-Transform_Thumbnail") 的 FilePreviewed 稽核記錄？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-535">**Could any non-user activities trigger FilePreviewed audit records that contain a user agent like "OneDriveMpc-Transform_Thumbnail"?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p175">我們不知道有什麼案例可使得非使用者動作產生類似這樣的事件。開啟使用者個人檔案卡片 (在 Outlook 網頁版的郵件中按一下其名稱或電子郵件地址) 之類的使用者動作會產生類似事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p175">We aren't aware of scenarios where non-user actions generate events like these. User actions like opening a user profile card (by clicking their name or email address in a message in Outlook on the web) would generate similar events.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-538">**對 OneDriveMpc-Transform_Thumbnail 的呼叫是否一律為使用者故意觸發？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-538">**Are calls to the OneDriveMpc-Transform_Thumbnail always intentionally being triggered by the user?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p176">不是。但類似事件可能由於瀏覽器預先擷取而加以記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p176">No. But similar events can be logged as a result of browser pre-fetch.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-541">**如果我們看到來自 Microsoft 註冊 IP 位址的 FilePreviewed 事件，則表示該預覽已在使用者裝置的螢幕上顯示了嗎？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-541">**If we see a FilePreviewed event coming from a Microsoft-registered IP address, does that mean that the preview was displayed on the screen of the user's device?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p177">不是。該事件可能由於瀏覽器預先擷取而加以記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p177">No. The event might have been logged as a result of browser pre-fetch.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-544">**是否有使用者預覽文件會產生 FileAccessed 事件的案例？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-544">**Are there scenarios where a user previewing a document generates FileAccessed events?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p178">FilePreviewed 和 FileAccessed 事件都表示使用者的呼叫導致讀取檔案 (或讀取檔案的縮圖呈現)。雖然這些事件旨在配合預覽與存取意圖，但事件差異並非使用者意圖的保證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p178">Both the FilePreviewed and FileAccessed events indicate that a user's call led to a read of the file (or a read of a thumbnail rendering of the file). While these events are intended to align with preview vs. access intention, the event distinction isn't a guarantee of the user's intent.</span></span>

#### <a name="the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-547">稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-547">The app\@sharepoint user in audit records</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p179">在部分檔案活動 (以及其他 SharePoint 相關活動) 的稽核記錄中，您可能會注意到執行活動的使用者 (User 和 UserId 欄位中識別) 為 app@sharepoint。這表示執行活動的「使用者」是應用程式。在此情況下，應用程式會獲授與 SharePoint 中的權限，以代表使用者、系統管理員或服務執行整個組織的動作 (例如搜尋 SharePoint 網站或 OneDrive 帳戶)。這種將權限授與應用程式的程序稱為 *僅限 SharePoint 應用程式* 存取權。這表示向 SharePoint 呈現，可執行動作的驗證是由應用程式 (而不是使用者) 所建立。這就是在特定稽核記錄中識別 app@sharepoint 使用者的原因。如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [使用僅限 SharePoint 應用程式授與存取權](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p179">In audit records for some file activities (and other SharePoint-related activities), you may notice the user who performed the activity (identified in the User and UserId fields) is app@sharepoint. This indicates that the "user" who performed the activity was an application. In this case, the application was granted permissions in SharePoint to perform organization-wide actions (such as search a SharePoint site or OneDrive account) on behalf of a user, admin, or service. This process of giving permissions to an application is called *SharePoint App-Only* access. This indicates that the authentication presented to SharePoint to perform an action was made by an application, instead of a user. This is why the app@sharepoint user is identified in certain audit records. For more information, see [Grant access using SharePoint App-Only](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p180">例如，app@sharepoint 通常會標示為「執行搜尋查詢」和「存取檔案」事件的使用者。這是因為當您將保留原則套用至網站和 OneDrive 帳戶時，組織中擁有僅限 SharePoint 應用程式存取權的應用程式會執行搜尋查詢和存取檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p180">For example, app@sharepoint is often identified as the user for "Performed search query" and "Accessed file" events. That's because an application with SharePoint App-Only access in your organization performs search queries and accesses files when applying retention policies to sites and OneDrive accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-557">以下是一些其他案例，其中 app@sharepoint 在稽核記錄中可能會識別為執行活動的使用者：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-557">Here are a few other scenarios where app@sharepoint may be identified in an audit record as the user who performed an activity:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p181">Microsoft 365 群組。當使用者或系統管理員建立新群組時，系統會產生稽核記錄，以建立網站集合、更新清單，以及將成員新增至 SharePoint 群組。這些工作是應用程式代表建立群組的使用者執行的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p181">Microsoft 365 Groups. When a user or admin creates a new group, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group. These tasks are performed an application on behalf of the user who created the group.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p182">Microsoft Teams。與 Microsoft 365 群組類似，建立新小組時，系統會產生稽核記錄，以建立網站集合、更新清單，以及將成員新增至 SharePoint 群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p182">Microsoft Teams. Similar to Microsoft 365 Groups, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group when a team is created.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p183">合規性功能。當系統管理員實作合規性功能時，例如保留原則、電子文件探索保留及自動套用敏感度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p183">Compliance features. When an admin implements compliance features, such as retention policies, eDiscovery holds, and auto-applying sensitivity labels.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p184">在這些及其他案例中，您也會注意到以 app@sharepoint 作為指定之使用者的稽核記錄是在短時間內建立的，彼此之間的間隔通常為幾秒鐘。這也表示這些稽核記錄可能是由相同使用者啟動的工作所觸發。此外，稽核記錄中的 ApplicationDisplayName 和 EventData 欄位可協助您識別觸發此事件的案例或應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p184">In these and other scenarios, you'll also notice that multiple audit records with app@sharepoint as the specified user were created within a short time frame, often within a few seconds of each other. This also indicates they were probably triggered by the same user-initiated task. Also, the ApplicationDisplayName and EventData fields in the audit record may help you identify the scenario or application that triggered the event.</span></span>

### <a name="folder-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-568">資料夾活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-568">Folder activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p185">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 的資料夾活動。如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p185">The following table describes the folder activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business. As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action. For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-572">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-572">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-573">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-573">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-574">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-574">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|

For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-678">共用及存取要求活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-678">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p192">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的使用者共用和存取要求活動。針對共用事件，[結果 **]** 底下的 [詳細資料 **]** 欄會識別共用項目的使用者或群組名稱，以及使用者或群組是否為您的組織中的成員或來賓。如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [在稽核記錄中使用共用稽核](use-sharing-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p192">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business. For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization. For more information, see [Use sharing auditing in the audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p193">根據使用者物件的 UserType 屬性，使用者可以是 *成員* 或 *來賓*。成員通常是員工，而來賓通常是貴組織之外的共同作業者。當使用者接受共用邀請時 (而且不屬於貴組織的一部分)，就會在貴組織目錄中為他們建立使用者帳戶。一旦來賓使用者在您的目錄中擁有帳戶後，就可以直接與他們共用資源 (而不需要邀請)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p193">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object. A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization. When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory. Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-686">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-686">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-687">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-687">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-688">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-688">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-689">已將權限等級新增至網站集合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-689">Added permission level to site collection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-690">PermissionLevelAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-690">PermissionLevelAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-691">權限等級已新增至網站集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-691">A permission level was added to a site collection.</span></span>|

In this case, the sharing invitation was blocked because: </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-704">允許的網域清單中不包含目標使用者的網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-704">The target user's domain isn't included in the list of allowed domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-705">或者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-705">Or</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-706">封鎖的網域清單中包含目標使用者的網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-706">The target user's domain is included in the list of blocked domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-707">如需根據網域允許或封鎖外部共用的詳細資訊，請參閱[在 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中限制網域共用](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/restricted-domains-sharing)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-707">For more information about allowing or blocking external sharing based on domains, see [Restricted domains sharing in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/restricted-domains-sharing).</span></span>|

### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-778">同步處理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-778">Synchronization activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-779">下表列出 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的檔案同步活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-779">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-780">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-780">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-781">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-781">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-782">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-782">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-783">已允許電腦同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-783">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-784">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-784">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p204">使用者與網站成功建立同步處理關聯性。成功同步處理關聯性是因為使用者的電腦為已新增至網域清單 (也稱為 *安全收件者清單*) 的網域之成員，而且加入此清單者可存取貴組織中的文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p204">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a site. The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the *safe recipients list*) that can access document libraries in your organization. </span></span><br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-787">如需有關此功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[使用 Windows PowerShell Cmdlet 為安全收件者清單上的網域啟用 OneDrive 同步處理](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-787">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-788">已阻擋電腦同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-788">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-789">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-789">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p205">使用者嘗試與網站建立同步處理關聯性，但該網站來自並非貴組織網域的成員或為未加入網域清單 (也稱為 *安全收件者清單*) 中網域的成員之電腦，而且加入此清單者可存取貴組織中的文件庫。不允許同步處理關聯性，並且禁止使用者的電腦在文件庫同步處理、下載或上傳檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p205">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list)*  that can access document libraries in your organization. The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library. </span></span><br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-792">如需此功能的相關資訊，請參閱[使用 Windows PowerShell Cmdlet 為安全收件者清單上的網域啟用 OneDrive 同步處理](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-792">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-793">已下載檔案至電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-793">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-794">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-794">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-795">使用者建立同步處理關聯性，且初次從文件庫成功下載檔案至電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-795">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer from a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-796">已下載檔案變更至電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-796">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-797">FileSyncDownloadedPartial </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-797">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p206">使用者從文件庫成功下載任何變更至檔案。此活動表示，對文件庫中的檔案所做之任何變更都已下載至使用者的電腦。因為使用者之前已下載文件庫，所以只會下載變更 (如 [已下載檔案至電腦] 活動所指出)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p206">User successfully downloads any changes to files from a document library. This activity indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer. Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the **Downloaded files to computer** activity).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-801">已下載檔案至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-801">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-802">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-802">FileSyncUploadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-803">使用者建立同步處理關聯性，且初次從電腦成功上傳檔案至文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-803">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads files for the first time from their computer to a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-804">已上傳檔案變更至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-804">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-805">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-805">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p207">使用者成功上傳變更至文件庫中的檔案。此事件表示，對來自文件庫的本機版本檔案所做的任何變更已成功上傳至文件庫。因為使用者之前已上傳這些檔案 (如 [已上傳檔案至文件庫 **]** 活動所指出)，所以只會上傳變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p207">User successfully uploads changes to files on a document library. This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library. Only changes are uploaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the **Uploaded files to document library** activity).</span></span>|

### <a name="site-permissions-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-809">網站權限活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-809">Site permissions activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p208">下表列出在 SharePoint 中指派權限及使用群組提供 (及撤銷) 網站存取權的相關事件。如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p208">The following table lists events related to assigning permissions in SharePoint and using groups to give (and revoke) access to sites. As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action. For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-816">已新增網站集合系統管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-816">Added site collection admin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-817">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-817">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p209">網站集合系統管理員擁有網站集合及所有子網站的完全控制權限。網站集合系統管理員擁有網站集合及所有子網站的完全控制權限。當系統管理員讓自己可存取使用者的 OneDrive 帳戶時 (藉由在 SharePoint 系統管理中心編輯使用者設定檔，或[使用 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data))，也會記錄此活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p209">Site collection administrator or owner adds a person as a site collection administrator for a site. ### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-877">網站管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-877">Site administration activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p218">下表列出 SharePoint Online 中的網站管理工作所產生的事件。如先前所述，某些 SharePoint 活動的稽核記錄將會指出 app@sharepoint 使用者代表啟動動作的使用者或系統管理員執行了動作。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核記錄中的 app\@sharepoint 使用者](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p218">The following table lists events that result from site administration tasks in SharePoint Online. As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action. For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-881">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-881">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-882">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-882">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-883">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-883">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-884">已新增允許的資料位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-884">Added allowed data location</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-885">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-885">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-886">SharePoint 或全域系統管理員已在多地理位置環境中新增允許的資料位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-886">A SharePoint or global administrator added an allowed data location in a multi-geo environment.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-887">已新增免除使用者代理程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-887">Added exempt user agent</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-888">ExemptUserAgentSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-888">ExemptUserAgentSet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-889">SharePoint 或全域系統管理員已將使用者代理程式新增至 SharePoint 系統管理員中心的免除使用者代理程式清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-889">A SharePoint or global administrator added a user agent to the list of exempt user agents in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span>|

||||

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-998">Exchange 信箱活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-998">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p233">下表列出信箱稽核記錄可以記錄的活動。信箱擁有者、指定使用者或管理員所執行的信箱活動會記錄在稽核記錄中達 90 天。系統管理員可能會關閉組織中所有使用者的信箱稽核記錄功能。在此情況下，任何使用者的信箱動作都不會記錄。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[管理信箱稽核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p233">The following table lists the activities that can be logged by mailbox audit logging. Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are automatically logged in the audit log for up to 90 days. It's possible for an admin to turn off mailbox audit logging for all users in your organization. In this case, no mailbox actions for any user are logged. For more information, see [Manage mailbox auditing](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1004">您也可以在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中使用 [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-mailboxauditlog) Cmdlet 來搜尋信箱活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1004">You can also search for mailbox activities by using the [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1005">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1005">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1006">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1006">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1007">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1007">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1008">存取信箱項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1008">Accessed mailbox items</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1009">MailItemsAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1009">MailItemsAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p234">已在信箱中讀取或存取郵件。可以通過以下兩種方式之一觸發此事件的稽核記錄：當郵件用戶端 (例如 Outlook) 對郵件執行繫結作業時，或者當郵件通訊協定 (例如 Exchange ActiveSync 或 IMAP) 同步郵件資料夾中的項目時。僅會對具備 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 E5 授權的使用者記錄此活動。在調查遭入侵的電子郵件帳戶時，分析此活動的稽核記錄相當實用。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[進階稽核](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations)中的＜存取調查重要事件＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p234">Messages were read or accessed in mailbox. Audit records for this activity are triggered in one of two ways: when a mail client (such as Outlook) performs a bind operation on messages or when mail protocols (such as Exchange ActiveSync or IMAP) sync items in a mail folder. This activity is only logged for users with an Office 365 or Microsoft 365 E5 license. Analyzing audit records for this activity is useful when investigating compromised email account. For more information, see the "Access to crucial events for investigations" section in [Advanced Audit](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations).</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1015">已新增代理人信箱權限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1015">Added delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1016">AddMailboxPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1016">AddMailboxPermissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p235">系統管理員已將另一名人員其信箱的 FullAccess 信箱權限指派給某個使用者 (亦稱為代理人)。FullAccess 權限可讓代理人開啟該名人員的信箱，以及讀取和管理信箱的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p235">An administrator assigned the FullAccess mailbox permission to a user (known as a delegate) to another person's mailbox. |<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1019">已新增或移除具有行事曆資料夾代理人存取權的使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1019">Added or removed user with delegate access to calendar folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1020">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1020">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p236">已新增或移除作為另一個使用者信箱行事曆代理人的使用者。行事曆代理可提供相同組織中的其他人權限來管理信箱擁有者的行事曆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p236">A user was added or removed as a delegate to the calendar of another user's mailbox. Calendar delegation gives someone else in the same organization permissions to manage the mailbox owner's calendar.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1023">已新增資料夾的權限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1023">Added permissions to folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1024">AddFolderPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1024">AddFolderPermissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p237">已新增資料夾權限。資料夾權限可控制組織中的哪些使用者可以存取信箱中的資料夾，以及這些資料夾中的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p237">A folder permission was added. ### <a name="user-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1097">使用者管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1097">User administration activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1098">下表列出當系統管理員透過 Microsoft 365 系統管理員中心或 Azure 管理入口網站新增或變更使用者帳戶時，會記錄的使用者管理活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1098">The following table lists user administration activities that are logged when an admin adds or changes a user account by using the Microsoft 365 admin center or the Azure management portal.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1099">活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1099">Activity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1100">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1100">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1101">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1101">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1102">已新增使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1102">Added user</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1103">新增使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1103">Add user</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1104">已建立使用者帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1104">A user account was created.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1105">已變更使用者授權</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1105">Changed user license</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1106">變更使用者授權</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1106">Change user license</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p247">指派給使用者的授權已變更。若要查看哪些授權已變更，請參閱對應的 [更新的使用者] 活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p247">The license assigned to a user what changed. ### <a name="ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1240">電子文件探索活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1240">eDiscovery activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p258">在安全性與合規性中心中或透過執行對應 PowerShell Cmdlet 所進行的內容搜尋和電子文件探索相關活動，會記錄在稽核記錄中。這包括下列活動：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p258">Content Search and eDiscovery-related activities that are performed in the security and compliance center or by running the corresponding PowerShell cmdlets are logged in the audit log. This includes the following activities:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1243">建立及管理電子文件探索案例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1243">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1244">建立、開啟及編輯 [內容搜尋]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1244">Creating, starting, and editing Content Searches</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1245">執行 [內容搜尋] 動作，例如預覽、匯出及刪除搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1245">Performing Content Search actions, such as previewing, exporting, and deleting search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1246">設定 [內容搜尋] 的權限篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1246">Configuring permissions filtering for Content Search</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="2358e-1247">管理電子文件探索系統管理員角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1247">Managing the eDiscovery Administrator role</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1248">如需已記錄電子文件探索活動的清單和詳細描述，請參閱[搜尋稽核記錄中的電子文件探索活動](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1248">For a list and detailed description of the eDiscovery activities that are logged, see [Search for eDiscovery activities in the audit log](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p259">[活動 **]** 下拉式清單中的 [電子文件探索活動 **]** 和 [進階文件探索活動 **]** 下方所列活動的結果事件，最久需要 30 分鐘才會顯示在搜尋結果中。相反地，系統需要 24 小時才能在搜尋結果中顯示電子文件探索 Cmdlet 活動的對應事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p259">It takes up to 30 minutes for events that result from the activities listed under **eDiscovery activities** and **Advanced eDiscovery activities** in the **Activities** drop-down list to be displayed in the search results. Conversely, it takes up to 24 hours for the corresponding events from eDiscovery cmdlet activities to appear in the search results.</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1254">Power BI 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1254">Power BI activities</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-workplace-analytics-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1260">Microsoft 工作場所分析活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1260">Microsoft Workplace Analytics activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p263">工作場所分析可針對群組在組織間共同作業的方式提供見解。下表列出在工作場所分析中獲指派系統管理員角色或分析師角色的使用者所執行的活動。獲指派分析師角色的使用者具有所有服務功能的完整存取權，並可使用產品來進行分析。獲指派系統管理員角色的使用者可以設定隱私權設定與系統預設值，並可以準備、上傳及驗證工作場所分析中的組織資料。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[工作場所分析](https://docs.microsoft.com/workplace-analytics/index-orig)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p263">Workplace Analytics provides insight into how groups collaborate across your organization. The following table lists activities performed by users that are assigned the Administrator role or the Analyst roles in Workplace Analytics. Users assigned the Analyst role have full access to all service features and use the product to do analysis. Users assigned the Administrator role can configure privacy settings and system defaults, and can prepare, upload, and verify organizational data in Workplace Analytics. For more information, see [Workplace Analytics](https://docs.microsoft.com/workplace-analytics/index-orig).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-teams-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1299">Microsoft Teams 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1299">Microsoft Teams activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p264">您可以在 Microsoft Teams 中搜尋使用者和系統管理員活動的稽核記錄。Teams 是 Office 365 中以聊天方式為主的工作區。它能將小組的交談、會議、檔案及筆記存放在同一個位置。如需受稽核的 Teams 活動描述，請參閱[在 Microsoft Teams 中搜尋事件的稽核記錄](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoftteams/audit-log-events#teams-activities)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p264">You can search the audit log for user and admin activities in Microsoft Teams. Teams is a chat-centered workspace in Office 365. It brings a team's conversations, meetings, files, and notes together into a single place. For descriptions of the Teams activities that are audited, see [Search the audit log for events in Microsoft Teams](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoftteams/audit-log-events#teams-activities).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-teams-healthcare-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1304">Microsoft Teams 醫療保健活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1304">Microsoft Teams Healthcare activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p265">如果貴組織正在 Microsoft Teams 中使用 [病患應用程式](https://docs.microsoft.com/MicrosoftTeams/expand-teams-across-your-org/healthcare/patients-app-overview)，則可以在稽核記錄中搜尋與病患應用程式相關的活動。如果您的環境設定為支援病患應用程式，則 **活動** 選擇器清單中提供了這些活動的其他活動群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p265">If your organization is using the [Patients application](https://docs.microsoft.com/MicrosoftTeams/expand-teams-across-your-org/healthcare/patients-app-overview) in Microsoft Teams, you can search the audit log for activities related to the using the Patients app. If your environment is configured to support Patients app, an additional activity group for these activities is available in the **Activities** picker list.</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-forms-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1422">Microsoft Forms 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1422">Microsoft Forms activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p278">下表列出稽核記錄中記錄的 Microsoft Forms 使用者和系統管理員活動。Microsoft Forms 是用來收集資料以進行分析的表單/測驗/問卷工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p278">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Microsoft Forms that are logged in the audit log. Microsoft Forms is a forms/quiz/survey tool used to collect data for analysis.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1425">以下說明中指出部分作業包含的其他活動參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1425">Where noted below in the descriptions, some operations contain additional activity parameters.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="2358e-p279">如果 Forms 活動是由共同作者或匿名回應者執行，則記錄方式會稍有不同。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[由共同作者和匿名回應者執行的 Forms 活動](#forms-activities-performed-by-coauthors-and-anonymous-responders)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p279">If a Forms activity is performed by a co-author or an anonymous responder, it will be logged slightly differently. For more information, see the [Forms activities performed by co-authors and anonymous responders](#forms-activities-performed-by-coauthors-and-anonymous-responders) section.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1524">已更新表單網路釣魚狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1524">Updated form phishing status</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1525">UpdatePhishingStatus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1525">UpdatePhishingStatus</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p287">每當內部安全性狀態的詳細資料值變更時，系統就會記錄此事件，無論這是否會變更最後的安全性狀態 (例如，現在已關閉或開啟表單)。這表示您可能會看到不具有最終安全性狀態變更的重複事件。此事件的可能狀態值如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p287">This event is logged whenever the detailed value for the internal security status was changed, regardless of whether this changed the final security state (for example, form is now Closed or Opened). This means you may see duplicate events without a final security state change. The possible status values for this event are:</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1529">- 記下</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1529">- Take Down</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1530">- 由系統管理員記下</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1530">- Take Down by Admin</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1531">- 系統管理員解除封鎖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1531">- Admin Unblocked</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1532">- 自動封鎖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1532">- Auto Blocked</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1533">- 自動解除封鎖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1533">- Auto Unblocked</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1534">- 客戶報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1534">- Customer Reported</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1535">- 重設客戶報告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1535">- Reset Customer Reported</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1536">更新的使用者網路釣魚狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1536">Updated user phishing status</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-1537">UpdateUserPhishingStatus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1537">UpdateUserPhishingStatus</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p288">每當使用者安全性狀態的值變更時，就會記錄此事件。當使用者建立的網路釣魚表單已由 Microsoft Online 安全小組記下，即會將稽核記錄中使用者狀態的值 **確認為網路釣魚者**。如果系統管理員解除封鎖該使用者，該使用者的狀態值會設定為 [重設為一般使用者 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p288">This event is logged whenever the value for the user security status was changed. The value of the user status in the audit record is **Confirmed as Phisher** when the user created a phishing form that was taken down by the Microsoft Online safety team. If an admin unblocks the user, the value of the user's status is set to **Reset as Normal User**.</span></span>|

#### <a name="forms-activities-performed-by-coauthors-and-anonymous-responders"></a><span data-ttu-id="2358e-1560">由共同作者和匿名回應者執行的 Forms 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-1560">Forms activities performed by coauthors and anonymous responders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2358e-p289">在設計表單和分析回應時，Forms 支援共同作業。表單共同作業者稱為 *共同作者*。在設計表單和分析回應時，Forms 支援共同作業。Forms 也可讓您建立可匿名回應的表單。這表示回應者不需要登入您的組織就能回應表單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2358e-p289">Forms supports collaboration when forms are designed and when analyzing responses. A form collaborator is known as a *coauthor*. Coauthors can do everything a form owner can do, except delete or move a form. Forms also allows you to create a form that can be responded to anonymously. This means the responder doesn't have to be signed into your organization to respond to a form.</span></span>
